# Filter out certain values from a list. #
let List.filter_map: (Int -> Int, [Int]) -> [Int] =
  fun f, xs ->
    case xs
    | [] => []
    | hd::tl =>
        let x = f(hd) in
        if x == 0 then List.filter_map(f, tl) else x::List.filter_map(f, tl)
